<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeve.html>groeve</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grove</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gruova</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōbō</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeve.html>groeve</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">groeyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gruoien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰreh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grow, become green</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***groen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>groen</a> (2146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:groene.html>groene</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gruoni</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*grōnī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōniz</i>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">grön</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">gröön</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">grün</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:grien.html>grien</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">green</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">grøn</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groenblauw.html>groenblauw</a> (105890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>groen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauw.html>blauw</a></i>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:groenblauw.html>groenblauw</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***groente.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a> (8278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groen.html>groen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groenten.html>groenten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groentes.html>groentes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groentje.html>groentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">groentetje</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Vegetables.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A (type of) vegetable.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>Groente</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> typically not used for a single piece of vegetable; instead that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a></i>. However, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a countable noun in both the singular and plural for a particular type (species, genus, cultivar, etc.) of vegetable.</li>
<li>While <i>groentetje</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the regular form of the diminutive, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not often used, likely because of its more difficult, less smooth pronunciation. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:groentje.html>Groentje</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the commonly used dimunitive.</li></ul>

***groep.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> (996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">gruppo</i>, though possibly borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">groupe</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krop.html>krop</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groepen.html>groepen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groepje.html>groepje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>group
<ul><li><b>1604</b>, Karel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Mander, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> schilder-boeck</i>, publ. by <a href = vnd.unilang:jacob.html>Jacob</a> Pietersz. <a href = vnd.unilang:wachter.html>Wachter</a> (print from 1618), page 112.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>Hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ſeer aerdich uytgebeeldt <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> grouwelijck Zee-onweder / daer oock <a href = vnd.unilang:noch.html>noch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schepen.html>Schepen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Schuyten vande <a href = vnd.unilang:felle.html>felle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>winden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevochten.html>bevochten</a> / ſeer <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> grooter aendacht ghedaen: ghelijck oock <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> eenen <b><a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:beelden.html>beelden</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> locht / in verſcheyden ghedaenten <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> quade gheeſten / <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:winden.html>Winden</a> blaſen / <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schip.html>Schip</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> raſende <a href = vnd.unilang:golven.html>golven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:riemen.html>riemen</a> crachtelijck wort geroeyt / <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beletten.html>beletten</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>circuit in an electrical installation, protected by a circuit breaker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In Belgium the word normally <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> the masculine gender. The feminine gender may still occur in formal Dutch from the Netherlands.
</p>

***groeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groeten.html>groeten</a> (1990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeten.html>groeten</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*gruoten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grōtijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groeten.html>groeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to greet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to salute</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begroeten.html>begroeten</a></span></li></ul>

***groezelig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:groezelig.html>groezelig</a> (60826)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">groes</i>, a eastern dialectal version of standard <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gruis.html>gruis</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gruis.html>gruis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grollen.html>grollen</a> (69765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:grollen.html>grollen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to debase; lower; humiliate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*<a href = vnd.unilang:grollen.html>grollen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gruljaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to yell; shout at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gellen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shout</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, compare <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grillen.html>grillen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shiver, shake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grill</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to provoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">growl</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gront</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">grunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grunduz</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grôot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">grōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grautaz</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootbrengen.html>grootbrengen</a> (17847)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big, great, adult</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grootbrengen.html>grootbrengen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To raise, bring up (a) young(<a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a>)(s), from infancy to maturity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To educate, rear, school, <a href = vnd.unilang:coach.html>coach</a> etc. offspring or other young <a href = vnd.unilang:charges.html>charges</a> on the path to adult life</li>
<li>the passive <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grootgebracht.html>grootgebracht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> means to grow up, mature (to majority)</li></ol>

***grootmoedig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootmoedig.html>grootmoedig</a> (23163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">great, grand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moedig.html>moedig</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tempered</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grot.html>grot</a> (3110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">grotta</i> or indirectly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">grotte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crypta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρυπτός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kruptós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:crypte.html>crypte</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">krocht</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gruft</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grotbewoner.html>grotbewoner</a> (117062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grot.html>grot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewoner.html>bewoner</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">inhabitant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grotbewoner.html>grotbewoner</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grotbewoners.html>grotbewoners</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One (human or animal) who inhabits a cave; a troglodyte.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This largely lacks the primitive and prehistoric connotations of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:holbewoner.html>holbewoner</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">caveman, troglodyte</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
</body>

***grouchy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a> (42216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>US 1895. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grouch</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>. Originally US college student <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">grouchier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">grouchiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">originally college <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Irritable; easily upset; angry; tending to complain. <span class="defdate">[From 1895]</span>
<dl><dd><i>His boss <a href = vnd.unilang:gets.html>gets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></b> when <a href = vnd.unilang:deadlines.html>deadlines</a> draw near.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1911</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jack_London" class="extiw" title="w:Jack London">London, <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a></a>,  chapter III, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Abysmal_Brute/Chapter_III" class="extiw" title="s:The Abysmal Brute/Chapter III">The Abysmal <a href = vnd.unilang:brute.html>Brute</a></a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Not that young Pat <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a nasty temper, or <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></b> as his father <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> feared.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sinclair_Lewis" class="extiw" title="w:Sinclair Lewis"><a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a>, Sinclair</a>,  chapter XXXI, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Babbitt/Chapter_31" class="extiw" title="s:Babbitt/Chapter 31">Babbitt</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> in to mumble that he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:sorry.html>sorry</a>, didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> mean to be <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></b>," and to inquire as to her interest in movies.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  Fischer, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> William,  “Author's Preface”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Abroad_with_Mark_Twain_and_Eugene_Field/Author%27s_Preface" class="extiw" title="s:Abroad with Mark Twain and Eugene Field/Author | s Preface">Abroad with Mark Twain and Eugene Field</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In Berlin I once <a href = vnd.unilang:heard.html>heard</a> Susie Clemens—ill-fated, talented girl, who died so young—say to her father: "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>Grouchy</a></b> again! They <i>do</i> say that you can be funny when company <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> around—too bad that you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> consider <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Fisher company."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cranky</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grumpy.html>grumpy</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tetchy</span>; See also Thesaurus:irritable</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***grumpy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:grumpy.html>grumpy</a> (49408)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">grump</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grumpy.html>grumpy</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">grumpier</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">grumpiest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Dissatisfied and irritable.
<dl><dd><i>The old <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:grumpy.html>grumpy</a></b> because he couldn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> find his glasses.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cantankerous</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">crabby</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cranky</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grouchy.html>grouchy</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">surly</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">truculent</span></li>
<li>See also Thesaurus:irritable</li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:grunge.html>grunge</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">grutte</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">gurte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*grutti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*grutją</i>.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gruwel.html>gruwel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horror</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.
